[30;1m503 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m504 | [0m[35mThis make Authentication classes more consistent:[0m
[30;1m505 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m506 | [0m[35m- OAuthTokenAuthentication is now a subclass of BasicTokenAuthentication (was Authentication)[0m
[30;1m507 | [0m[35m- BasicTokenAuthentication has now a "set_token" methods that does nothing.[0m
